name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in August 2022
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted August 13, 2022
msg:Suichang, a county with a long history in southwestern Zhejiang. I had never heard of this place 3 days ago. 3 days later, when the child waved goodbye to Zhang Ying, the customer service manager, he shouted through the car window: I must come back again.
Yes, Tom Radisson, how can a three-night stay?
As a senior tourist, I have lived in the ancient castle for a hundred years, and I have also lived in the Rongbu Temple with broken sheets at the foot of *************. Tanggong Radisson is a very attentive hotel. Everyone who works here is humble, professional and enthusiastic. From the piety of the customer service manager Miss Zhang, who bends over and puts on her shoes, to the gift from Hu Zhean at the front desk to the child, and an unknown person in the restaurant. The staff who wear a suit and want to refill my coffee make people feel at home. This is the hotel with the most considerate service I have seen in China in the three years since the epidemic. I feel like I went to a hot spring hotel in the mountains of Japan when they line up until you can't see them.
Because the newly renovated hotel hardware is particularly comfortable, from toothbrushes, to smart toilets, smart curtains, bedding, towels, bathrobes, slippers, air conditioning, and even sinks, faucets, and showers. Every detail about comfort can be taken into account by the operator.
Let's talk about breakfast: breakfast is quite hearty, not only many varieties but also very delicious, local special prune cakes are freshly baked, as well as various kinds of kuey teow (similar to rice cakes), freshly cut Jinhua ham, salmon, children The happiest, pizza ice cream fries, the coffee here is the most variety I have ever seen in a hotel. As a heavy coffee lover, it is very satisfying to drink two cups every morning.
The infinity swimming pool is a beautiful landscape. The path leading to the swimming pool is full of flowers and plants, and it is carefully maintained by the hotel staff early in the morning. The swimming pool is 1.35 meters deep, suitable for adults and children.
Yes, as the child said, where you live and live again, this is a place worthy of your special visit.
In my opinion, it has achieved the ceiling of the hotel's cost-effectiveness.

posted:Posted August 8, 2022
msg:advantage:
1. Traffic location: Get off at the Suichang exit of Lining Expressway and go straight for about 8 minutes. It's convenient to go anywhere.
2. The hotel just opened in July 2022, and the facilities are very new.
3. There are many varieties of breakfast, which is very good.
4. There is an open-air infinity pool.
shortcoming:
1. Newly opened hotel, slightly decorated, sensitive people should be cautious
2. The breakfast is very good. However, 98 yuan is still a little expensive, 58-68 is more suitable
3. The mattress is very soft. This varies from person to person. Not too obvious a disadvantage.
4. After staying for 3 nights, I found that the cleaning is limited to the bedding, and the bathroom supplies are supplemented. It seems that the floor is not swept.
Overall it is OK, the first choice for accommodation in Suichang.
